======================================================================
NAVMESH TASKLET PRESSURE CONTRACT AUDIT
======================================================================

Question this script tries to answer:
  Did the pathfinding/navmesh tasklet path allocate or consume optional arrays

  Registers at crash had EAX=ECX=4 and EDX=NavMeshInfoSearch.
